\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
\begin{Indent}\textbf{ Client side interaction}\par
{\em These methods allow to activate the client side interactive features of a W\+Cartesian\+Chart.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Client side interaction is only available if the chart is drawn on an H\+T\+ML canvas. This is the default rendering method on modern browsers, see \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPaintedWidget_a18d1ee409a269274335d377fb17ba74d}{W\+Painted\+Widget\+::set\+Preferred\+Method()}}

Some features are currently not supported in interactive mode\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Axes set at \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga77eb6d0cefa4a012950ea972b471b849ad7ed4ee1df437474d005188535f74875}{Axis\+Value\+::\+Zero}} position will not always be drawn correctly. They may be clipped off outside of the chart area, and when zooming, the axis ticks will change size.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis_a159f74342b4800e5c5be11eb1b2a351b}{W\+Axis\+::set\+Break()}} is incompatible with interactive mode 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A cartesian chart. 

A cartesian chart is a chart that uses X and Y axes. It can display one or multiple data series, which each may be rendered using bars, lines, areas, or points.

To use a cartesian chart, the minimum you need to do is set a model using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAbstractChart_a2243e89c5ee56f48da4b1ca49e854c0f}{set\+Model()}}, set the model column that holds the X data using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a6c954fa4ed6d73f00ee973bfe3af5ed0}{set\+X\+Series\+Column(int model\+Column)}}, and add one or more series using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ade295a3e179a0e83dd608b0dfc54372a}{add\+Series(std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$\+W\+Data\+Series$>$)}}. Each series corresponds to one data column that holds Y data.

A cartesian chart is either a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}} or a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa09870720ca8134284e4e305ac6ce5f19}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Scatter}}.

In a {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}}}}, the X series represent different categories, which are listed consecutively in model row order. The X axis scale is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggadfcaed8cd6ff52f5747f7df48f2eeab6a4984667940802dedc139aa7a430a6553}{Axis\+Scale\+::\+Discrete}}.



Each series may be rendered differently, and this is configured in the data series (see \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} for more information).

In a {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa09870720ca8134284e4e305ac6ce5f19}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Scatter}}}}, the X series data are interpreted as numbers on a numerical scale. The scale for the X axis defaults to a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggadfcaed8cd6ff52f5747f7df48f2eeab6a32a843da6ea40ab3b17a3421ccdf671b}{Axis\+Scale\+::\+Linear}}, but this may be changed to a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggadfcaed8cd6ff52f5747f7df48f2eeab6a44749712dbec183e983dcd78a7736c41}{Axis\+Scale\+::\+Date}} when the X series contains dates (of type \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WDate}{W\+Date}}) to create a time series chart, or to a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggadfcaed8cd6ff52f5747f7df48f2eeab6ace0be71e33226e4c1db2bcea5959f16b}{Axis\+Scale\+::\+Log}}. A \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa09870720ca8134284e4e305ac6ce5f19}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Scatter}} supports the same types of data series as a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}}, but does not support stacking. In a scatter plot, the X series do not need to be ordered in increasing values, and may be set differently for each dataseries using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries_a9361e12e94699f59090ae8ac3a4921df}{W\+Data\+Series\+::set\+X\+Series\+Column(int model\+Column)}}.



Missing data in a model series Y values is interpreted as a {\itshape break}. For curve-\/like series, this breaks the curve (or line).

The cartesian chart has support for dual Y axes. Each data series may be bound to one of the two Y axes. By default, only the first Y axis is displayed. To show the second Y axis you will need to call\+:

By default a chart has a horizontal X axis and a vertical Y axis, which corresponds to a \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Orientation\+::\+Vertical}} orientation. The orientation may be changed to \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Orientation\+::\+Horizontal}} using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ac8638a7ae6b0d1141794d9c07336e500}{set\+Orientation()}}.

The styling of the series data are dictated by a palette which may be set using set\+Palette(\+W\+Chart\+Palette $\ast$), but may be overridden by settings in each data series.

\doxyparagraph*{C\+SS}

Styling through C\+SS is not applicable.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addSeries()}{addSeries()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::add\+Series (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} $>$}]{series }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Adds a data series. 

A single chart may display one or more data series. Each data series displays data from a single model column in the chart. Series are plotted in the order that they have been added to the chart.

The series column is reset to -\/1 when the model is set (or changed). Thus you need to set a model before configuring the series.

\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!initLayout@{initLayout}}
\index{initLayout@{initLayout}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{initLayout()}{initLayout()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::init\+Layout (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WRectF}{W\+RectF}} \&}]{rectangle = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WRectF}{W\+RectF}}()},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPaintDevice}{W\+Paint\+Device}} $\ast$}]{device = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Initializes the chart layout. 

The mapping between model and device coordinates is only established after a rendering phase, or after calling init\+Layout manually.

You need a layout in order to use the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afa6f3b2c0851a335998c69a13c30db3c}{map\+From\+Device()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a146820fa83f208f588a24c2ffd0e9ede}{map\+To\+Device()}} methods.

Unless a specific chart rectangle is specified, the entire widget area is assumed. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae8265e6c80d5c0d73863ae623165cb3d}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae8265e6c80d5c0d73863ae623165cb3d}}

Returns whether this chart is interactive.

\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!mapFromDevice@{mapFromDevice}}
\index{mapFromDevice@{mapFromDevice}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mapFromDevice()}{mapFromDevice()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::map\+From\+Device (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} \&}]{point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9f}{Axis}}}]{ordinate\+Axis = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9fa5d32a72e2819aaf62362fcc862b37c5e}{Axis\+::\+Ordinate}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Maps from device coordinates to model coordinates. 

Maps a position in the chart back to model coordinates.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

If the chart is interactive, map\+From\+Device will correctly take the current zoom range into account.

Maps a position in the chart back to model coordinates.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

If the chart is interactive, map\+From\+Device will correctly take the current zoom range into account.

Maps a position in the chart back to model coordinates.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

If the chart is interactive, map\+From\+Device will correctly take the current zoom range into account.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a89c8de50cf89b4fc11e47c6b3a1eb438}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a89c8de50cf89b4fc11e47c6b3a1eb438}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform@{mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform}}
\index{mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform@{mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform()}{mapFromDeviceWithoutTransform()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::map\+From\+Device\+Without\+Transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} \&}]{point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9f}{Axis}}}]{ordinate\+Axis = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9fa5d32a72e2819aaf62362fcc862b37c5e}{Axis\+::\+Ordinate}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Maps from device coordinates to model coordinates, ignoring the current zoom range. 

Maps a position in the chart back to model coordinates, as if the chart was not zoomed in (nor panned).

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

This function will not take the current zoom range into account. The mapping will be performed as if \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a913934a771968399273449ce789a0423}{zoom\+Range\+Transform()}} is the identity transform.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Maps from device coordinates to model coordinates, ignoring the current zoom range. 

Maps a position in the chart back to model coordinates, as if the chart was not zoomed in (nor panned).

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

This function will not take the current zoom range into account. The mapping will be performed as if \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a913934a771968399273449ce789a0423}{zoom\+Range\+Transform()}} is the identity transform.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

This function will not take the current zoom range into account. The mapping will be performed as if \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a913934a771968399273449ce789a0423}{zoom\+Range\+Transform()}} is the identity transform.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a146820fa83f208f588a24c2ffd0e9ede}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a146820fa83f208f588a24c2ffd0e9ede}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!mapToDevice@{mapToDevice}}
\index{mapToDevice@{mapToDevice}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mapToDevice()}{mapToDevice()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::map\+To\+Device (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classlinb_1_1any}{cpp17\+::any}} \&}]{x\+Value,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classlinb_1_1any}{cpp17\+::any}} \&}]{y\+Value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9f}{Axis}}}]{axis = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ggaddb678f67fbd9f374fcee0922f158c9fa5d32a72e2819aaf62362fcc862b37c5e}{Axis\+::\+Ordinate}}},  }\item[{int}]{x\+Segment = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{int}]{y\+Segment = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Maps model values onto chart coordinates. 

This returns the chart device coordinates for a (x,y) pair of model values.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. If you have not yet rendered the chart, or wish that the mapping already reflects model changes since the last rendering, you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afb8c75682293611eace3d5899a03eb07}{init\+Layout()}} first.

The {\ttfamily x\+Segment} and {\ttfamily y\+Segment} arguments are relevant only when the corresponding axis is broken using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis_a159f74342b4800e5c5be11eb1b2a351b}{W\+Axis\+::set\+Break()}}. Then, its possible values may be 0 (below the break) or 1 (above the break).

If the chart is interactive, map\+To\+Device will correctly take the current zoom range into account.

This uses the axis dimensions that are based on the latest chart rendering. \index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!removeXAxis@{removeXAxis}}
\index{removeXAxis@{removeXAxis}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeXAxis()}{removeXAxis()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis}{W\+Axis}}$>$ Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::remove\+X\+Axis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{x\+Axis\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Removes the X axis with the given id. 

The indices of the axes with an id higher than x\+Axis\+Id will be decremented.

Any \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} associated with the removed axis are also removed.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Precondition\+: 0 $<$= x\+Axis\+Id $<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a64777980578bb25de7074c20ba26904e}{x\+Axis\+Count()}} 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aaea1755116b75cb5959d69b1b3c4baed}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aaea1755116b75cb5959d69b1b3c4baed}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!removeYAxis@{removeYAxis}}
\index{removeYAxis@{removeYAxis}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeYAxis()}{removeYAxis()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis}{W\+Axis}}$>$ Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::remove\+Y\+Axis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{y\+Axis\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Removes the Y axis with the given id. 

The indices of the axes with an id higher than y\+Axis\+Id will be decremented.

Any \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} associated with the removed axis are also removed.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Precondition\+: 0 $<$= y\+Axis\+Id $<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a2650a9fae3f660196b32bcfd30b90386}{y\+Axis\+Count()}} 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aab19ac7fa211d60dfa64808e882fc866}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aab19ac7fa211d60dfa64808e882fc866}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!render@{render}}
\index{render@{render}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{render()}{render()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::render (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFlags}{W\+Flags}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a1097ddb5b58c20fe2f6c9d096e71575c}{Render\+Flag}} $>$}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Renders the widget. 

This function renders the widget (or an update for the widget), after this has been scheduled using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget_a5d3d4edaafa2d7c892a5078f3df4cf11}{schedule\+Render()}}.

The default implementation will render the widget by serializing changes to Java\+Script and H\+T\+ML. You may want to reimplement this widget if you have been postponing some of the layout / rendering implementation until the latest moment possible. In that case you should make sure you call the base implementation however. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPaintedWidget_ab268e85a9ecfb97c9a743a1f9c5ec6c9}{Wt\+::\+W\+Painted\+Widget}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::render (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter}{W\+Painter}} \&}]{painter,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WRectF}{W\+RectF}} \&}]{rectangle }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Renders the chart. 

Renders the chart within the given rectangle. To accomodate both rendering of horizontal and vertically oriented charts, all rendering logic assumes horizontal. This \char`\"{}chart coordinates\char`\"{} space is transformed to painter coordinates using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a4d1023156ed68ea1e5eaff2e6eccad9e}{hv()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a29495fcf00762662f8a44c72c8732be1}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a29495fcf00762662f8a44c72c8732be1}}

\index{renderLabel@{renderLabel}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renderLabel()}{renderLabel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::render\+Label (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter}{W\+Painter}} \&}]{painter,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WString}{W\+String}} \&}]{text,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} \&}]{pos,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFlags}{W\+Flags}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_ab8f772c69bc8180c31f9e4f4593b143f}{Alignment\+Flag}} $>$}]{flags,  }\item[{double}]{angle,  }\item[{int}]{margin }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Utility function for rendering text. 

This method renders text on the chart position {\itshape pos}, with a particular alignment {\itshape flags}. These are both specified in chart coordinates. The position is converted to painter coordinates using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a4d1023156ed68ea1e5eaff2e6eccad9e}{hv()}}, and the alignment flags are changed accordingly. The rotation, indicated by {\itshape angle} is specified in painter coordinates and thus an angle of 0 always indicates horizontal text, regardless of the chart orientation. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afdb09f7b8de08a4a1f50920bb8040201}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_afdb09f7b8de08a4a1f50920bb8040201}}

Renders the legend icon for a given data series. 

Renders the legend icon for the indicated {\ttfamily series} in the {\ttfamily painter} at position {\ttfamily pos}.

This method is called while rendering a legend item, and you may want to reimplement this method if you wish to provide a custom legend icon for a particular data series.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a3a4abe9cf1f503799d343b3056760d1f}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a3a4abe9cf1f503799d343b3056760d1f}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renderLegendItem()}{renderLegendItem()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::render\+Legend\+Item (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter}{W\+Painter}} \&}]{painter,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPointF}{W\+PointF}} \&}]{pos,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} \&}]{series }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Renders the legend item for a given data series. 

Renders the legend item for the indicated {\ttfamily series} in the {\ttfamily painter} at position {\ttfamily pos}. The default implementation draws the marker, and the series description to the right. The series description is taken from the model\textquotesingle{}s header data for that series\textquotesingle{} data column.

This method is called while painting the chart, and you may want to reimplement this method if you wish to provide a custom marker for a particular data series.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aa15c2965b1a5423e7c7a958629ea2057}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aa15c2965b1a5423e7c7a958629ea2057}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!renderOther@{renderOther}}
\index{renderOther@{renderOther}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renderOther()}{renderOther()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::render\+Other (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter}{W\+Painter}} \&}]{painter }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Renders other, user-\/defined things. 

The default implementation sets the painter\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter_a65be44d995c5f06f065f68d15c8889a5}{clip path}} to the chart area, but does not enable clipping.

This method can be overridden to draw extra content onto the chart.

Chart coordinates can be mapped to device coordinates with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a9aaa4e422196e3ef33ed4dad98299195}{map\+To\+Device\+Without\+Transform()}}. If these need to move and scale along with the zoom range, those points can be transformed with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a913934a771968399273449ce789a0423}{zoom\+Range\+Transform()}}.

This method is called last by default. If you want to render other things at some other moment, you can override render(\+W\+Painter\&, const W\+Rect\+F\&). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ade46b3158562160b5a68787ddab7c98f}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ade46b3158562160b5a68787ddab7c98f}}

A signal that notifies the selection of a new curve. 

This signal is emitted if a series is selected using a mouse click or long press. The first argument is the selected series. The second argument is the point that was selected, in model coordinates.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Bar\+Margin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{margin }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the margin between bars of different series. 

Use this method to change the margin that is set between bars of different series. The margin is specified as a fraction of the width. For example, a value of 0.\+1 adds a 10\% margin between bars of each series. Negative values are also allowed. For example, use a margin of -\/1 to plot the bars of different series on top of each other.

The default value is 0. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_acf9fb3b059aff07a63b45215929843df}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_acf9fb3b059aff07a63b45215929843df}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Crosshair\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{crosshair = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables the crosshair functionality. 

When enabled, the crosshair will follow mouse movement, and show in the top right corner the coordinate (according to X axis and the first Y axis) corresponding to this position.

When using touch, the crosshair can be moved with a drag. If both panning and the crosshair are enabled, the crosshair will be moved when dragging close to the crosshair. Otherwise, the chart will pan. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aef10bf73dc30c2fab92aedc6f9ff586b}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aef10bf73dc30c2fab92aedc6f9ff586b}}

W\+Data\+Series\+::selected\+Series() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a7941c22269e9b9aa30b2d9c31289860e}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a7941c22269e9b9aa30b2d9c31289860e}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setFollowCurve@{setFollowCurve}}
\index{setFollowCurve@{setFollowCurve}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFollowCurve()}{setFollowCurve()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Follow\+Curve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} $\ast$}]{series }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enabled the follow curve funtionality for a data series. 

This enables follow curve functionality for the data series corresponding to the given column.

If the data series is of type \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a4803e6b9e63dabf04de980788d6a13c4}{Series\+Type\+::\+Line}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a2cb4d4a3f8dacd623fa045a44febd476}{Series\+Type\+::\+Curve}}, the crosshair can only be moved in the x direction. The y position of the crosshair will be determined by the value of the data series. The crosshair will snap to the nearest point that is defined in the data series.

When using the mouse, the x position will change on mouseover. When using touch, the x position can be moved with a drag. The follow curve functionality has priority over the crosshair functionality.

Set to null to disable the follow curve feature.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The follow curve functionality requires that the X axis values of the data series are monotonically increasing or decreasing. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a2a3c3c567c2d2e10effeac70dc0cdb4d}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a2a3c3c567c2d2e10effeac70dc0cdb4d}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setFollowCurve@{setFollowCurve}}
\index{setFollowCurve@{setFollowCurve}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFollowCurve()}{setFollowCurve()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Follow\+Curve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{model\+Column }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables the follow curve functionality for a data series. 

This enables follow curve functionality for the data series corresponding to the given column.

If the data series is of type \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a4803e6b9e63dabf04de980788d6a13c4}{Series\+Type\+::\+Line}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a2cb4d4a3f8dacd623fa045a44febd476}{Series\+Type\+::\+Curve}}, the crosshair can only be moved in the x direction. The y position of the crosshair will be determined by the value of the data series. The crosshair will snap to the nearest point that is defined in the data series.

When using the mouse, the x position will change on mouseover. When using touch, the x position can be moved with a drag. The follow curve functionality has priority over the crosshair functionality.

Use column index -\/1 or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aac7673c7c38d7d98383bee7b72ae556d}{disable\+Follow\+Curve()}} to disable the follow curve feature.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The follow curve functionality requires that the X axis values of the data series are monotonically increasing or decreasing.
\end{DoxyNote}

\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000009}{Deprecated}}]Use \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a7941c22269e9b9aa30b2d9c31289860e}{set\+Follow\+Curve(const W\+Data\+Series$\ast$)}} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a9f4133ef8280991032bded06ce2dc58a}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a9f4133ef8280991032bded06ce2dc58a}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setLegendColumns@{setLegendColumns}}
\index{setLegendColumns@{setLegendColumns}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLegendColumns()}{setLegendColumns()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Legend\+Columns (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{columns,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WLength}{W\+Length}} \&}]{width }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configures multiple legend columns. 

Multiple columns are typically useful when placing the legend at the top or at the bottom of the chart.

The default value is a single column, 100 pixels wide.

When automatic chart layout is enabled, then the legend column width is computed automatically, and this setting is ignored.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAbstractChart_ac895fb1d1437f51629b49246eda66e3d}{set\+Auto\+Layout\+Enabled()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a26c3d97f4884da079e01e7b50447a915}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a26c3d97f4884da079e01e7b50447a915}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setLegendEnabled@{setLegendEnabled}}
\index{setLegendEnabled@{setLegendEnabled}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLegendEnabled()}{setLegendEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Legend\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables the legend. 

The location of the legend can be configured using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae4336637c800631714ec521cbf2aa452}{set\+Legend\+Location()}}. Only series for which the legend is enabled are included in this legend.

The default value is {\ttfamily false}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries_af74437aa169d754271080b5a33cb3d91}{W\+Data\+Series\+::is\+Legend\+Enabled()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae4336637c800631714ec521cbf2aa452}{set\+Legend\+Location()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae4336637c800631714ec521cbf2aa452}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ae4336637c800631714ec521cbf2aa452}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setLegendLocation@{setLegendLocation}}
\index{setLegendLocation@{setLegendLocation}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLegendLocation()}{setLegendLocation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Legend\+Location (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ga950e490e52f40d945b7301bf3831f2af}{Legend\+Location}}}]{location,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a5a6f4636bcc6ab3c075165d249b3a5a3}{Side}}}]{side,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_ab8f772c69bc8180c31f9e4f4593b143f}{Alignment\+Flag}}}]{alignment }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configures the legend location. 

The legend can be renderd either inside or outside of the chart area. When {\ttfamily location} is \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga950e490e52f40d945b7301bf3831f2afa9b6d3000134648fc9f1e71094ae0847d}{Chart\+::\+Legend\+Location\+::\+Inside}}, the legend will be rendered inside the chart. When {\ttfamily location} is \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga950e490e52f40d945b7301bf3831f2afa76fbf0ccd7fcd64879c2ff2119dc15a4}{Chart\+::\+Legend\+Location\+::\+Outside}}, the legend is rendered outside the chart, in the chart padding area.

The provided {\ttfamily side} can either be Wt\+::\+Side\+::\+Left, Wt\+::\+Side\+::\+Right, Wt\+::\+Side\+::\+Top, Wt\+::\+Side\+::\+Bottom and configures the side of the chart at which the legend is displayed.

The {\ttfamily alignment} specifies how the legend is aligned. This can be a horizontal alignment flag (Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Left, Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Center, or Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Right), when the {\ttfamily side} is Side\+::\+Bottom or Side\+::\+Top, or a vertical alignment flag (Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Top, Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Middle, or Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Bottom) when the {\ttfamily side} is Side\+::\+Left or Side\+::\+Right.

The default location is \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga950e490e52f40d945b7301bf3831f2afa76fbf0ccd7fcd64879c2ff2119dc15a4}{Chart\+::\+Legend\+Location\+::\+Outside}}, Wt\+::\+Side\+::\+Right and Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Middle.

To have more control over the legend, you could reimplement the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a3a4abe9cf1f503799d343b3056760d1f}{render\+Legend\+Item()}} method to customize how one item in the legend is rendered, or, alternatively you can disable the legend generated by the chart itself, and reimplement the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a6d39c5541205ae168279f52698e0260e}{paint()}} method in which you use the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a3a4abe9cf1f503799d343b3056760d1f}{render\+Legend\+Item()}} method repeatedly to render a customized legend.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries_adbddd50fc4ccd1608987900f0231bd50}{W\+Data\+Series\+::set\+Legend\+Enabled()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a94505b419f2ed8ba4d939de57944397d}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a94505b419f2ed8ba4d939de57944397d}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setLegendStyle@{setLegendStyle}}
\index{setLegendStyle@{setLegendStyle}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLegendStyle()}{setLegendStyle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Legend\+Style (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFont}{W\+Font}} \&}]{font,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPen}{W\+Pen}} \&}]{border,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WBrush}{W\+Brush}} \&}]{background }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configures the legend decoration. 

This configures the font, border and background for the legend.

The default font is a 10pt sans serif font (the same as the default axis label font), the default {\ttfamily border} is \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Pen\+Style\+::\+None}} and the default {\ttfamily background} is \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Brush\+Style\+::\+None}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a97f7f38a9f751b0b41d67f4546cc32f9}{set\+On\+Demand\+Loading\+Enabled()}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_aad195b4918cb5039054b05c00e236032}{loading\+Background()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a97f7f38a9f751b0b41d67f4546cc32f9}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a97f7f38a9f751b0b41d67f4546cc32f9}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setOnDemandLoadingEnabled@{setOnDemandLoadingEnabled}}
\index{setOnDemandLoadingEnabled@{setOnDemandLoadingEnabled}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setOnDemandLoadingEnabled()}{setOnDemandLoadingEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+On\+Demand\+Loading\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable on-\/demand loading. 

By default, when on-\/demand loading is not enabled, the entire chart area is loaded, regardless of whether it is within the current zoom range of the X axis.

When on-\/demand loading is enabled only the currently visible area + some margin is loaded. As the visible area changes, different data is loaded. This improves performance for charts with a lot of data if not all of the data needs to be visible at the same time.

This feature is especially useful in combination with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis_ada743ccf44212cfb1f4a6fa83b79e581}{W\+Axis\+::set\+Maximum\+Zoom\+Range()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis_a13d7f38a677d502e3b5dd0d9550e6d33}{W\+Axis\+::set\+Min\+Zoom()}}, which makes it impossible for the user to view all of the data at the same time, because that would incur too much overhead.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On-\/demand loading requires that the X axis data for all data series is sorted in ascending order. This feature is optimized for equidistant X axis data, but that\textquotesingle{}s not a requirement.

If no minimum or maximum are set on the Y axis (or axes), then the chart will still have to scan all data of its data series to automatically determine the minimum and maximum Y axis values. If this performance hit is undesirable and the Y axis range is known or guaranteed to be within a certain range, make sure to \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis_aae563fd94b81a03cfe2662dbde2ae548}{set a range}} on the Y axis (or axes).
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_acd3549734d554765bcbcc698ea15eece}{on\+Demand\+Loading\+Enabled()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ac8638a7ae6b0d1141794d9c07336e500}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_ac8638a7ae6b0d1141794d9c07336e500}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setOrientation@{setOrientation}}
\index{setOrientation@{setOrientation}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setOrientation()}{setOrientation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Orientation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a2a8d45559e16a0185bf61bfad0a67912}{Orientation}}}]{orientation }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the chart orientation. 

Sets the chart orientation, which corresponds to the orientation of the Y axis\+: a Wt\+::\+Orientation\+::\+Vertical orientation corresponds to the conventional way of a horizontal X axis and vertical Y axis. A Wt\+::\+Orientation\+::\+Horizontal orientation is the other way around.

The default orientation is Wt\+::\+Orientation\+::\+Vertical.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a4bb5996032ffc1ff28f87b4200a68623}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a4bb5996032ffc1ff28f87b4200a68623}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setPanEnabled@{setPanEnabled}}
\index{setPanEnabled@{setPanEnabled}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPanEnabled()}{setPanEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Pan\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{pan = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables pan functionality. 

When using the mouse, you can click and drag to pan the chart (if zoomed in), or use the scrollwheel.

When using touch, you can drag to pan the chart. If the rubberband effect is enabled, this is intertial (it will keep scrolling after you let go) and there is an overscroll and bounce back effect on the sides.

The default value is {\ttfamily false}.

\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setSelectedSeries@{setSelectedSeries}}
\index{setSelectedSeries@{setSelectedSeries}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSelectedSeries()}{setSelectedSeries()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Selected\+Series (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}} $\ast$}]{series }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the series that is currently selected. 

The series with the given model column will be selected. The other series will be shown in a lighter color. The series that is currently selected is the one that can be manipulated if \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a6078b67f146e686bd482d846dfe463cb}{curve manipulation}} is enabled, and it is a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a4803e6b9e63dabf04de980788d6a13c4}{Series\+Type\+::\+Line}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a2cb4d4a3f8dacd623fa045a44febd476}{Series\+Type\+::\+Curve}}.

The selected series can be changed using a long touch or mouse click.

If the argument provided is null or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a8fdd621fa64e84ca7e95e67b617dd63f}{series selection}} is not enabled, no series will be selected.

Sets whether series selection is enabled. 

If series selection is enabled, series can be selected with a mouse click or long press. If the selected series is a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a4803e6b9e63dabf04de980788d6a13c4}{Series\+Type\+::\+Line}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga44d64e4a9d08c7ef69648f4a9c3e4053a2cb4d4a3f8dacd623fa045a44febd476}{Series\+Type\+::\+Curve}}, it can be manipulated if \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a6078b67f146e686bd482d846dfe463cb}{curve manipulation}} is enabled. The series that are not selected, will be shown in a lighter color. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a2f400f8b923fec8ba5140a42d94dda23}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a2f400f8b923fec8ba5140a42d94dda23}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a02775290965d59ffba03da574925e387}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a02775290965d59ffba03da574925e387}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setType@{setType}}
\index{setType@{setType}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setType()}{setType()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_ga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfea}{Chart\+Type}}}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the chart type. 

The chart type determines how (x,y) data are interpreted. In a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}}, the X values are categories, and these are plotted consecutively, evenly spaced, and in row order. In a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa09870720ca8134284e4e305ac6ce5f19}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Scatter}}, the X values are interpreted numerically (as for Y values).

The default chart type is a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}}.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setXSeriesColumn@{setXSeriesColumn}}
\index{setXSeriesColumn@{setXSeriesColumn}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setXSeriesColumn()}{setXSeriesColumn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+X\+Series\+Column (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{model\+Column }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the the model column for the X series. 

Use this method to specify the default data for the X series. For a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa09870720ca8134284e4e305ac6ce5f19}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Scatter}} this is mandatory if an X series is not specified for every \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries}{W\+Data\+Series}}. For a \mbox{\hyperlink{group__charts_gga8d63464f873580c77508e1c0c26cbfeaa3adbdb3ac060038aa0e6e6c138ef9873}{Chart\+Type\+::\+Category}}, if not specified, an increasing series of integer numbers will be used (1, 2, ...).

Scatterplot dataseries may each individually be given its own X series data using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WDataSeries_a9361e12e94699f59090ae8ac3a4921df}{W\+Data\+Series\+::set\+X\+Series\+Column(int model\+Column)}}

The default value is -\/1 (not specified).

The series column is reset to -\/1 when the model is set (or changed). Thus you need to set a model before configuring the series.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a08e3ff107e45b85bbd277db217850185}{X\+Series\+Column()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a5ff1331e2837807cae16fea146e93ce4}\label{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a5ff1331e2837807cae16fea146e93ce4}} 
\index{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}!setZoomEnabled@{setZoomEnabled}}
\index{setZoomEnabled@{setZoomEnabled}!Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart@{Wt::Chart::WCartesianChart}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setZoomEnabled()}{setZoomEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::set\+Zoom\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{zoom = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables zoom functionality. 

When using the mouse, press the ctrl key while scrolling to zoom in/out a specific point on the chart. If you press shift+ctrl, it will only zoom vertically. If you press alt+ctrl, it will only zoom horizontally. To change these default mappings, use \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a9080d0351171802250889d1dd5e3ae92}{set\+Wheel\+Actions()}}.

When using touch, you can use a pinch gesture to zoom in/out. If the pinch gesture is vertical/horizontal, it will zoom only vertically/horizontally, otherwise it will zoom both axes equally.

The default value is {\ttfamily false}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesianChart_a6d39c56a38cbc91952aea4b617ce1a2d}{zoom\+Enabled()}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{zoomRangeTransform()}{zoomRangeTransform()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WTransform}{W\+Transform}} Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian\+Chart\+::zoom\+Range\+Transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis}{W\+Axis}} \&}]{x\+Axis,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WAxis}{W\+Axis}} \&}]{y\+Axis }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}



Returns the current zoom range transform. 

This transform maps device coordinates from the fully zoomed out position to the current zoom range.

This transform is a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WJavaScriptExposableObject_a4e121ccbb14715c33dc1b019b6636156}{Java\+Script bound}} transform if this chart is interactive. Otherwise, this transform is just the identity transform.

Returns the current zoom range transform. 

This transform maps device coordinates from the fully zoomed out position to the current zoom range.

This transform is a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WJavaScriptExposableObject_a4e121ccbb14715c33dc1b019b6636156}{Java\+Script bound}} transform if this chart is interactive. Otherwise, this transform is just the identity transform.
